<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwik.html>kwik</a> (16817)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwikzilver.html>kwikzilver</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwik.html>kwik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>the element mercury</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thermometer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kwik.html>kwik</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vannacht.html>vannacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> nul <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaald.html>gedaald</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Temperatures</b> have decreased to below zero (centigrade) tonight.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">quic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">quic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kwikwaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">quick</i>.
</p>

***laag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laag.html>laag</a> (1968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lâge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lāgi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lēgaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laag.html>laag</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>lager</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laagst.html>laagst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>low
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laag.html>laag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:tafeltje.html>tafeltje</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woonkamer.html>woonkamer</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>low</b> table in his living room.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nogal.html>nogal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laag.html>laag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diegene.html>diegene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verder.html>verder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It's rather <b>low</b> to attack someone on issues they don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have any control <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laak.html>laak</a> (128089)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lake</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:laka.html>laka</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lakō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drain, ditch, stream, pool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*leǵ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to leak, drain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laak.html>laak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laken.html>laken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laak.html>laakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:pond.html>pond</a>, pool, lake</li>

<li>A drainage ditch.</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lāke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blood sucking worm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lieke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>leke</a></i>, from a root shared with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lēkijaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">leech</i>.

***laar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laar.html>laar</a> (37003)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">laer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lāri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lēziz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lēzijaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></i>, obsolete English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lere.html>lere</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laar.html>laar</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laar.html>laarder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laarzen.html>laarst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> empty</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">laer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lār</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hlār</i> (only in place names), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlēraz</i> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlēzaz</i>. The etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear, and the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> in the languages where it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> found, in any case. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hlār</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hlār</i>, both only on place names.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laar.html>laar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laar.html>laren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laar.html>laartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> open space in a forest</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">leerse</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">laerse</i>, from syncope of unattested *<i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lederse</i>, contracted from *<i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lederhose</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hose</i>. </p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-, second- and third-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">laet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lāt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lētaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">serf</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatst.html>laatst</a> (1166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Superlative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a></i></span></li>
<li>latest, most recent, newest</li>
<li>last, furthest behind</li>
<li>final, ultimate</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laatst.html>laatst</a></strong>

***labeur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:labeur.html>labeur</a> (103972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:labeur.html>labeur</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:labeur.html>labeur</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">labor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">labor</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:labeur.html>labeur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> toil, hard labour, heavy labour, in the past esp. on agricultural <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

***labyrint.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:labyrint.html>labyrint</a> (19383)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">labyrinthus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λαβύρινθος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">labúrinthos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">maze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly from an Anatolian language (compare Lydian <i>lábrus</i> 'double-edged axe' and <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a><i>inthos</i>, a suffix typical of Anatolian placenames), although the actual etymology of <i>labyrinth</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still a matter of conjecture.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:labyrint.html>labyrint</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:labyrinten.html>labyrinten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:labyrint.html>labyrintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">labyrinth</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">maze</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> intricate problem, logic etc.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doolhof.html>doolhof</a></span></li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:labyrint.html>labyrint</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stelsel.html>stelsel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paden.html>paden</a> of dwaalwegen, <a href = vnd.unilang:zodanig.html>zodanig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aangelegd.html>aangelegd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarin.html>daarin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeilijk.html>moeilijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a></li></ol>

***lachen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lachen.html>lachen</a> (881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lachen.html>lachen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lahhan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hlahjaną</i>.
</p>

***lachrymose.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lachrymose.html>lachrymose</a> (81953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lacrimōsus</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lacrima</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-osus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Old Latin">Old Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="itc-ola">dacrima</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dakru-</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tear</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lachrymose.html>lachrymose</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:lachrymose.html>lachrymose</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:lachrymose.html>lachrymose</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Tearful, sorrowful, sad, pertaining to <a href = vnd.unilang:tears.html>tears</a>, weeping, causing <a href = vnd.unilang:tears.html>tears</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:crying.html>crying</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1927</b>,  Thornton <a href = vnd.unilang:wilder.html>Wilder</a>,  <cite>The Bridge of San <a href = vnd.unilang:luis.html>Luis</a> Rey</cite>, page 69:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> true that Limeans <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> given to interpolating trivial <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a> into the most exquisite comedies and some <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lachrymose.html>lachrymose</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:effects.html>effects</a> into the austerest music; but at least they never submitted to the boredom of a misplaced veneration.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lachrymatory</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lachrymosely</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lachrymosity</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">unlachrymose</span></li></ul>

***lachspiegel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lachspiegel.html>lachspiegel</a> (103963)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lachen.html>lachen</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lach.html>lach</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spiegel.html>spiegel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lachspiegel.html>lachspiegel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lachspiegel.html>lachspiegels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lachspiegel.html>lachspiegeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>distorting mirror</li></ol>

***lackey.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lackey.html>lackey</a> (103961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">laquais</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably (<a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">lacai</i>?) from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">lacayo</i>, itself perhaps from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">lacchè</i> and <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">λακές</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lakés</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">ulak</i>. Another possibility <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> through <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catalan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Catalan language">Catalan</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ca">alacay</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">اَلْقَاضِي</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">al-qāḍī</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">magistrate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">laquais</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lackey.html>lackey</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lackeys</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A footman, a liveried male servant.
<ul><li><b>1820</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Maturin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Maturin">Charles Maturin</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Melmoth_the_Wanderer" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Melmoth the Wanderer">Melmoth the Wanderer</a></i>, volume 1, page 198:
<dl><dd>My <a href = vnd.unilang:dearest.html>dearest</a> father,—I say nothing of them,—but <i>I dare</i> to speak of myself,—I can never be a monk,—if that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> your object—spurn <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>,—order your <b>lacqueys</b> to drag <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> from this carriage,—leave <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> a beggar in the streets to cry “<i>fire and water</i>,”—but do not make <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> a monk.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1884</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Ruskin" class="extiw" title="w:John Ruskin">John Ruskin</a>,  “By the Rivers of Waters”, in  <cite>“Our <a href = vnd.unilang:fathers.html>Fathers</a> Have <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>Told</a> Us.”: <a href = vnd.unilang:sketches.html>Sketches</a> of the History of <a href = vnd.unilang:christendom.html>Christendom</a> for Boys and <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>Girls</a> who have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>Held</a> at Its Fonts</cite>, part I (The Bible of Amiens), Orpington, <a href = vnd.unilang:kent.html>Kent</a> |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Allen_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:George Allen (publisher)">George <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>Allen</a></a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/222616845">222616845</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/ourfathershaveto00ruskpage/30/mode/2up">pages 30–31</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">St. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martin_of_Tours" class="extiw" title="w:Martin of Tours">Martin [of Tours]</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:looks.html>looks</a> round, first, deliberately;—becomes aware of a tatterdemalion and thirsty-looking soul of a beggar at his chair side, who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> managed to get <i>his</i> cup filled somehow, also—by a charitable <b>lacquey</b>. St. Martin turns his back on the Empress, and hobnobs with <i>him</i>!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A fawning, servile follower.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">lickspittle</span>; <i>see also</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">loyal follower</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lackey.html>lackey</a> caterpillar</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lackey.html>lackey</a> moth</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lackey.html>lackey</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">lackeys</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lackeying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lackeyed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To attend, wait upon, serve obsequiously.
<ul><li><b>ca. 1607</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:antony.html>Antony</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:cleopatra.html>Cleopatra</a></i>, Act I, sc. 3:
<dl><dd>[<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>]he ebbed <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, ne'<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loved.html>loved</a> till ne'<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> worth love,</dd>
<dd><a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>Comes</a> deared by being lacked. This common body,</dd>
<dd>Like to a vagabond flag upon the stream,</dd>
<dd>Goes to and back, <b>lackeying</b> the varying tide,</dd>
<dd>To <a href = vnd.unilang:rot.html>rot</a> itself with motion.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1634</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Milton">John Milton</a>. <i>Comus</i>:
<dl><dd>So dear to Heav'n <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Saintly chastity,</dd>
<dd>That when a soul <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> found sincerely so,</dd>
<dd>A thousand liveried Angels <b>lacky</b> her ...</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To toady, play the flunky.</li></ol>

***lager.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>lager</a> (3769)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>Lager</a></i>; doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leger.html>leger</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>lager</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lagers.html>lagers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>lagertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bearing <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a metal block or other construction holding a rotating axis in position</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kegellager</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kogellager.html>kogellager</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>Lager</a></i>, shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lagerbier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>lager</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>Lager</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">camp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>Bier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>lager</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lagers.html>lagers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>lagertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a> of low fermentation</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>Lager</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">camp, encampment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with semantic influence from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans"><a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af">laer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lager.html>lager</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lagers.html>lagers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> laager <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">wagon fort used by <a href = vnd.unilang:boers.html>Boers</a>, especially Voortrekkers</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***lain.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lain.html>lain</a> (91394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inflected forms.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lain.html>lain</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be oriented in a horizontal position, situated</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lain.html>lain</a></b> there for many <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>The book <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lain.html>lain</a></b> on the attic floor until it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> found decades <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tell a lie, not tell a truth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lied.html>lied</a></i>.</li>
<li>The past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lay</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">put down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">laid</i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lainen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">leynen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">leyna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to conceal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">līeġnan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to deny; conceal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laugnijaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laugnō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">secrecy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lain.html>lain</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">lains</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">laining</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lained</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To conceal, keep quiet about. <span class="defdate">[14<sup>th</sup>-19<sup>th</sup>c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1485</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Malory" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Malory">Thomas Malory</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://quod.lib.umich.edu/c/cme/MaloryWks2/1:22.1?rgn=div2;view=fulltext">chapter j</a>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Le_Morte_d%27Arthur" class="extiw" title="w:Le Morte d | Arthur">Le <a href = vnd.unilang:morte.html>Morte</a> Darthur</a></i>, book XX:
<dl><dd>Also broder <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a> Agrauayne and <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a> mordred in lyke wyse <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a> Launcelot rescowed <a href = vnd.unilang:yow.html>yow</a> bothe and thre score and two from <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a> Turquyn / <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>Me</a> thynketh broder suche kynde dedes and kyndenes shold be remembryd / <a href = vnd.unilang:doo.html>doo</a> as ye lyst sayd syr Agrauayne for I wylle <b><a href = vnd.unilang:layne.html>layne</a></b> it no lenger</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***lak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lak.html>lak</a> (12538)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First occurring in the late 16th century. Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">laque</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">لاک</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lāk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">लाख</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lākh</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">लाक्षा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lākṣā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lak.html>lak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lakken.html>lakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lak.html>lakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">lacquer</span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lac.html>lac</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laka-</i>, related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lak.html>lak</a>(k)ōn-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blame, reproach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lok-néh₂-</i>.  See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">lakr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lacking</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lak.html>lak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lakken.html>lakken</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">defect</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">deficiency</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">shortcoming</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">blame</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">blemish</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lac.html>lac</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:laka.html>laka</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*laku</i>.
</p>

***lakei.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lakei.html>lakei</a> (28109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lackey.html>lackey</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">laquais</i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp">lacayo</i>, of uncertain origin; cognate with <a href = vnd.unilang:lackey.html>lackey</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lakei.html>lakei</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lakeien.html>lakeien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lakei.html>lakeitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:lackey.html>lackey</a>, a footman, a liveried servant, an attendant.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">livreibediende</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">livreiknecht</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A flunky, servile follower.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaafje.html>slaafje</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voetveeg.html>voetveeg</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lakei.html>lakei</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lakei.html>lakei</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:dienaar.html>dienaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bediende.html>bediende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkend.html>werkend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koninklijk.html>koninklijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a>.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:gewone.html>gewone</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huishoudens.html>huishoudens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lakei.html>lakei</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekend.html>bekend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Engelse <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:butler.html>butler</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lakeien.html>lakeien</a> (37002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lakeien.html>lakeien</a></strong>

***laken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laken.html>laken</a> (10114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lāken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lakan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lakaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">linen, cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laken.html>laken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lakens.html>lakens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laken.html>lakentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a type of woollen fabric, very sought-after for clothing in the feudal era (uncountable)</li>
<li>bedsheet</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">lakenhal</span></li>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">lakenhoes</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">lakenlood</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">lakenscheerder</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">lakenstempel</span></li></ul></div><div class="list-switcher-element" data-showtext=" show more ▼ " data-hidetext=" show less  " style="display: none;"> </div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lāken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lak.html>lak</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to criticize, reproach, denounce
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gasten.html>gasten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groezelig.html>groezelig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>motel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:laken.html>laken</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:tevergeefs.html>tevergeefs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebrekkige.html>gebrekkige</a> hygiëne <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lakens.html>lakens</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The guests in that sleazy <a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>motel</a> denounce in vain the poor sheets hygiene</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lam.html>lam</a> (5943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lam.html>lam</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lamb</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lambaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lam.html>lam</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lammeren.html>lammeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lammetje.html>lammetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lamb, the young of a sheep</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The meat <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> or fleece/wool produce of a lamb; a dish prepared from lamb's meat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A gentle person, especially an innocent child</li></ol>

***lamia.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lamia.html>lamia</a> (56912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:lamia.html>lamia</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Λάμια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Lámia</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lamia.html>lamia</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lamias</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lamiae</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Greek mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a> preying upon human beings and who sucked the blood of children, often described as having the head and breasts of a woman and the lower <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of a serpent.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1624</b>,  Democritus <a href = vnd.unilang:junior.html>Junior</a> [pseudonym; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Burton_(scholar)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Burton (scholar)">Robert Burton</a>],  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Anatomy_of_Melancholy" class="extiw" title="w:The Anatomy of Melancholy">The Anatomy of Melancholy | <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="What It Is. With All the Kindes, Cavses, Symptomes, Prognosticks, and Seuerall Cvres of It. In Three Maine Partitions, with Their Seuerall Sections, Members, and Svbsections. Philosophically, Medicinally, Historically Opened and Cut Up, by Democritvs Junior, with a Satyricall Preface, Conducing to the Following Discourse">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, 2nd edition, Oxford, Oxfordshire |  Printed by John Lichfield and James Short, for <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Cripps, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/54573970">54573970</a></small>, partition III, section 2, member 1, subsection i:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Apollonius <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> by some probable conjectures, found her out to be a serpent, a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lamia.html>lamia</a></b>, and that all her furniture <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> like Tantalus' gold described by <a href = vnd.unilang:homer.html>Homer</a>, no substance, but <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a> illusions.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">vampire</span></li></ul>

***lamp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a> (3700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lampe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">lampe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lampas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a>; torch; lantern</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λαμπάς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lampás</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">torch; <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λάμπω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lámpō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*leh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lampen.html>lampen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lampje.html>lampje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a></a></li>
